<s> THE LOST WORLD The Lost World CHAPTER I "There Are Heroisms All Round Us" Mr Hungerton, her father, really was the most tactless person upon earth,--a fluffy, feathery, untidy cockatoo of a man, perfectly good-natured, but absolutely centered upon his own silly self </s>
<s> If anything could have driven me from Gladys, it would have been the thought of such a father-in-law </s>
<s> I am convinced that he really believed in his heart that I came round to the Chestnuts three days a week for the pleasure of his company, and very especially to hear his views upon bimetallism, a subject upon which he was by way of being an authority </s>
<s> For an hour or more that evening I listened to his monotonous chirrup about bad money driving out good, the token value of silver, the depreciation of the rupee, and the true standards of exchange </s>
<s> "Suppose," he cried with feeble violence, "that all the debts in the world were called up simultaneously, and immediate payment insisted upon,--what under our present conditions would happen then" </s>
<s> I gave the self-evident answer that I should be a ruined man, upon which he jumped from his chair, reproved me for my habitual levity, which made it impossible for him to discuss any reasonable subject in my presence, and bounced off out of the room to dress for a Masonic meeting </s>
<s> At last I was alone with Gladys, and the moment of Fate had come </s>

<s> How beautiful she was </s>
<s> And yet how aloof </s>

<s> When we arrived at the hall we found a much greater concourse than I had expected </s>
<s> A line of electric broughams discharged their little cargoes of white-bearded professors, while the dark stream of humbler pedestrians, who crowded through the arched door-way, showed that the audience would be popular as well as scientific </s>

<s> The uproar of his advent had not yet died away when Professor Ronald Murray, the chairman, and Mr Waldron, the lecturer, threaded their way to the front, and the proceedings began </s>
<s> Professor Murray will, I am sure, excuse me if I say that he has the common fault of most Englishmen of being inaudible </s>
<s> Why on earth people who have something to say which is worth hearing should not take the slight trouble to learn how to make it heard is one of the strange mysteries of modern life </s>
<s> Their methods are as reasonable as to try to pour some precious stuff from the spring to the reservoir through a non-conducting pipe, which could by the least effort be opened </s>
<s> Professor Murray made several profound remarks to his white tie and to the water-carafe upon the table, with a humorous, twinkling aside to the silver candlestick upon his right </s>
<s> Then he sat down, and Mr Waldron, the famous popular lecturer, rose amid a general murmur of applause </s>
<s> He was a stern, gaunt man, with a harsh voice, and an aggressive manner, but he had the merit of knowing how to assimilate the ideas of other men, and to pass them on in a way which was intelligible and even interesting to the lay public, with a happy knack of being funny about the most unlikely objects, so that the precession of the Equinox or the formation of a vertebrate became a highly humorous process as treated by him </s>
<s> It was a bird's-eye view of creation, as interpreted by science, which, in language always clear and sometimes picturesque, he unfolded before us </s>
<s> He told us of the globe, a huge mass of flaming gas, flaring through the heavens </s>
<s> Then he pictured the solidification, the cooling, the wrinkling which formed the mountains, the steam which turned to water, the slow preparation of the stage upon which was to be played the inexplicable drama of life </s>
<s> On the origin of life itself he was discreetly vague </s>
<s> That the germs of it could hardly have survived the original roasting was, he declared, fairly certain </s>
<s> Therefore it had come later </s>
<s> Had it built itself out of the cooling, inorganic elements of the globe </s>
<s> Very likely </s>
<s> Had the germs of it arrived from outside upon a meteor </s>
<s> It was hardly conceivable </s>
<s> On the whole, the wisest man was the least dogmatic upon the point </s>
<s> We could not--or at least we had not succeeded up to date in making organic life in our laboratories out of inorganic materials </s>
<s> The gulf between the dead and the living was something which our chemistry could not as yet bridge </s>
<s> But there was a higher and subtler chemistry of Nature, which, working with great forces over long epochs, might well produce results which were impossible for us </s>
<s> There the matter must be left </s>
<s> This brought the lecturer to the great ladder of animal life, beginning low down in molluscs and feeble sea creatures, then up rung by rung through reptiles and fishes, till at last we came to a kangaroo-rat, a creature which brought forth its young alive, the direct ancestor of all mammals, and presumably, therefore, of everyone in the audience </s>
<s> ("No, no," from a sceptical student in the back row.) If the young gentleman in the red tie who cried "No, no," and who presumably claimed to have been hatched out of an egg, would wait upon him after the lecture, he would be glad to see such a curiosity </s>
<s> (Laughter.) It was strange to think that the climax of all the age-long process of Nature had been the creation of that gentleman in the red tie </s>
<s> But had the process stopped </s>
<s> Was this gentleman to be taken as the final type--the be-all and end-all of development </s>

<s> Evolution was not a spent force, but one still working, and even greater achievements were in store </s>

<s> CHAPTER VI "I was the Flail of the Lord" Lord John Roxton and I turned down Vigo Street together and through the dingy portals of the famous aristocratic rookery </s>
<s> At the end of a long drab passage my new acquaintance pushed open a door and turned on an electric switch </s>
<s> A number of lamps shining through tinted shades bathed the whole great room before us in a ruddy radiance </s>
<s> Standing in the doorway and glancing round me, I had a general impression of extraordinary comfort and elegance combined with an atmosphere of masculine virility </s>
<s> Everywhere there were mingled the luxury of the wealthy man of taste and the careless untidiness of the bachelor </s>
<s> Rich furs and strange iridescent mats from some Oriental bazaar were scattered upon the floor </s>
<s> Pictures and prints which even my unpractised eyes could recognize as being of great price and rarity hung thick upon the walls </s>
<s> Sketches of boxers, of ballet-girls, and of racehorses alternated with a sensuous Fragonard, a martial Girardet, and a dreamy Turner </s>
<s> But amid these varied ornaments there were scattered the trophies which brought back strongly to my recollection the fact that Lord John Roxton was one of the great all-round sportsmen and athletes of his day </s>
<s> A dark-blue oar crossed with a cherry-pink one above his mantel-piece spoke of the old Oxonian and Leander man, while the foils and boxing-gloves above and below them were the tools of a man who had won supremacy with each </s>
<s> Like a dado round the room was the jutting line of splendid heavy game-heads, the best of their sort from every quarter of the world, with the rare white rhinoceros of the Lado Enclave drooping its supercilious lip above them all </s>
<s> In the center of the rich red carpet was a black and gold Louis Quinze table, a lovely antique, now sacrilegiously desecrated with marks of glasses and the scars of cigar-stumps </s>
<s> On it stood a silver tray of smokables and a burnished spirit-stand, from which and an adjacent siphon my silent host proceeded to charge two high glasses </s>
<s> Having indicated an arm-chair to me and placed my refreshment near it, he handed me a long, smooth Havana </s>
<s> Then, seating himself opposite to me, he looked at me long and fixedly with his strange, twinkling, reckless eyes--eyes of a cold light blue, the color of a glacier lake </s>
<s> Through the thin haze of my cigar-smoke I noted the details of a face which was already familiar to me from many photographs--the strongly-curved nose, the hollow, worn cheeks, the dark, ruddy hair, thin at the top, the crisp, virile moustaches, the small, aggressive tuft upon his projecting chin </s>
<s> Something there was of Napoleon III., something of Don Quixote, and yet again something which was the essence of the English country gentleman, the keen, alert, open-air lover of dogs and of horses </s>
<s> His skin was of a rich flower-pot red from sun and wind </s>
<s> His eyebrows were tufted and overhanging, which gave those naturally cold eyes an almost ferocious aspect, an impression which was increased by his strong and furrowed brow </s>
<s> In figure he was spare, but very strongly built--indeed, he had often proved that there were few men in England capable of such sustained exertions </s>
<s> His height was a little over six feet, but he seemed shorter on account of a peculiar rounding of the shoulders </s>
<s> Such was the famous Lord John Roxton as he sat opposite to me, biting hard upon his cigar and watching me steadily in a long and embarrassing silence </s>
<s> "Well," said he, at last, "we've gone and done it, young fellah my lad" </s>

<s> I am writing these last lines in the saloon of the Booth liner Francisca, and they will go back by the pilot to the keeping of Mr McArdle </s>
<s> Let me draw one last picture before I close the notebook--a picture which is the last memory of the old country which I bear away with me </s>
<s> It is a wet, foggy morning in the late spring; a thin, cold rain is falling </s>
<s> Three shining mackintoshed figures are walking down the quay, making for the gang-plank of the great liner from which the blue-peter is flying </s>

<s> CHAPTER VII "To-morrow we Disappear into the Unknown" I will not bore those whom this narrative may reach by an account of our luxurious voyage upon the Booth liner, nor will I tell of our week's stay at Para (save that I should wish to acknowledge the great kindness of the Pereira da Pinta Company in helping us to get together our equipment) </s>
<s> I will also allude very briefly to our river journey, up a wide, slow-moving, clay-tinted stream, in a steamer which was little smaller than that which had carried us across the Atlantic </s>
<s> Eventually we found ourselves through the narrows of Obidos and reached the town of Manaos </s>
<s> Here we were rescued from the limited attractions of the local inn by Mr Shortman, the representative of the British and Brazilian Trading Company </s>
<s> In his hospital Fazenda we spent our time until the day when we were empowered to open the letter of instructions given to us by Professor Challenger </s>
<s> Before I reach the surprising events of that date I would desire to give a clearer sketch of my comrades in this enterprise, and of the associates whom we had already gathered together in South America </s>
<s> I speak freely, and I leave the use of my material to your own discretion, Mr McArdle, since it is through your hands that this report must pass before it reaches the world </s>
<s> The scientific attainments of Professor Summerlee are too well known for me to trouble to recapitulate them </s>
<s> He is better equipped for a rough expedition of this sort than one would imagine at first sight </s>
<s> His tall, gaunt, stringy figure is insensible to fatigue, and his dry, half-sarcastic, and often wholly unsympathetic manner is uninfluenced by any change in his surroundings </s>
<s> Though in his sixty-sixth year, I have never heard him express any dissatisfaction at the occasional hardships which we have had to encounter </s>
<s> I had regarded his presence as an encumbrance to the expedition, but, as a matter of fact, I am now well convinced that his power of endurance is as great as my own </s>
<s> In temper he is naturally acid and sceptical </s>
<s> From the beginning he has never concealed his belief that Professor Challenger is an absolute fraud, that we are all embarked upon an absurd wild-goose chase and that we are likely to reap nothing but disappointment and danger in South America, and corresponding ridicule in England </s>
<s> Such are the views which, with much passionate distortion of his thin features and wagging of his thin, goat-like beard, he poured into our ears all the way from Southampton to Manaos </s>
<s> Since landing from the boat he has obtained some consolation from the beauty and variety of the insect and bird life around him, for he is absolutely whole-hearted in his devotion to science </s>
<s> He spends his days flitting through the woods with his shot-gun and his butterfly-net, and his evenings in mounting the many specimens he has acquired </s>
<s> Among his minor peculiarities are that he is careless as to his attire, unclean in his person, exceedingly absent-minded in his habits, and addicted to smoking a short briar pipe, which is seldom out of his mouth </s>
<s> He has been upon several scientific expeditions in his youth (he was with Robertson in Papua), and the life of the camp and the canoe is nothing fresh to him </s>
<s> Lord John Roxton has some points in common with Professor Summerlee, and others in which they are the very antithesis to each other </s>
<s> He is twenty years younger, but has something of the same spare, scraggy physique </s>
<s> As to his appearance, I have, as I recollect, described it in that portion of my narrative which I have left behind me in London </s>
<s> He is exceedingly neat and prim in his ways, dresses always with great care in white drill suits and high brown mosquito-boots, and shaves at least once a day </s>
<s> Like most men of action, he is laconic in speech, and sinks readily into his own thoughts, but he is always quick to answer a question or join in a conversation, talking in a queer, jerky, half-humorous fashion </s>
<s> His knowledge of the world, and very especially of South America, is surprising, and he has a whole-hearted belief in the possibilities of our journey which is not to be dashed by the sneers of Professor Summerlee </s>
<s> He has a gentle voice and a quiet manner, but behind his twinkling blue eyes there lurks a capacity for furious wrath and implacable resolution, the more dangerous because they are held in leash </s>
<s> He spoke little of his own exploits in Brazil and Peru, but it was a revelation to me to find the excitement which was caused by his presence among the riverine natives, who looked upon him as their champion and protector </s>
<s> The exploits of the Red Chief, as they called him, had become legends among them, but the real facts, as far as I could learn them, were amazing enough </s>
<s> These were that Lord John had found himself some years before in that no-man's-land which is formed by the half-defined frontiers between Peru, Brazil, and Columbia </s>
<s> In this great district the wild rubber tree flourishes, and has become, as in the Congo, a curse to the natives which can only be compared to their forced labor under the Spaniards upon the old silver mines of Darien </s>
<s> A handful of villainous half-breeds dominated the country, armed such Indians as would support them, and turned the rest into slaves, terrorizing them with the most inhuman tortures in order to force them to gather the india-rubber, which was then floated down the river to Para </s>
<s> Lord John Roxton expostulated on behalf of the wretched victims, and received nothing but threats and insults for his pains </s>
<s> He then formally declared war against Pedro Lopez, the leader of the slave-drivers, enrolled a band of runaway slaves in his service, armed them, and conducted a campaign, which ended by his killing with his own hands the notorious half-breed and breaking down the system which he represented </s>
<s> No wonder that the ginger-headed man with the silky voice and the free and easy manners was now looked upon with deep interest upon the banks of the great South American river, though the feelings he inspired were naturally mixed, since the gratitude of the natives was equaled by the resentment of those who desired to exploit them </s>
<s> One useful result of his former experiences was that he could talk fluently in the Lingoa Geral, which is the peculiar talk, one-third Portuguese and two-thirds Indian, which is current all over Brazil </s>
<s> I have said before that Lord John Roxton was a South Americomaniac </s>
<s> He could not speak of that great country without ardor, and this ardor was infectious, for, ignorant as I was, he fixed my attention and stimulated my curiosity </s>
<s> How I wish I could reproduce the glamour of his discourses, the peculiar mixture of accurate knowledge and of racy imagination which gave them their fascination, until even the Professor's cynical and sceptical smile would gradually vanish from his thin face as he listened </s>
<s> He would tell the history of the mighty river so rapidly explored (for some of the first conquerors of Peru actually crossed the entire continent upon its waters), and yet so unknown in regard to all that lay behind its ever-changing banks </s>
<s> "What is there" </s>
<s> he would cry, pointing to the north </s>
<s> "Wood and marsh and unpenetrated jungle </s>
<s> Who knows what it may shelter </s>
<s> And there to the south </s>
<s> A wilderness of swampy forest, where no white man has ever been </s>
<s> The unknown is up against us on every side </s>
<s> Outside the narrow lines of the rivers what does anyone know </s>
<s> Who will say what is possible in such a country </s>
<s> Why should old man Challenger not be right" </s>
<s> At which direct defiance the stubborn sneer would reappear upon Professor Summerlee's face, and he would sit, shaking his sardonic head in unsympathetic silence, behind the cloud of his briar-root pipe </s>

<s> But already we have enrolled certain retainers who may play no small part in what is to come </s>
<s> The first is a gigantic negro named Zambo, who is a black Hercules, as willing as any horse, and about as intelligent </s>

<s> One of them, Gomez, had the further advantage that he could speak excellent English </s>

<s> Besides these, we had engaged three Mojo Indians from Bolivia, who are the most skilful at fishing and boat work of all the river tribes </s>
<s> The chief of these we called Mojo, after his tribe, and the others are known as Jose and Fernando </s>
<s> Three white men, then, two half-breeds, one negro, and three Indians made up the personnel of the little expedition which lay waiting for its instructions at Manaos before starting upon its singular quest </s>
<s> At last, after a weary week, the day had come and the hour </s>
<s> I ask you to picture the shaded sitting-room of the Fazenda St </s>
<s> Ignatio, two miles inland from the town of Manaos </s>
<s> Outside lay the yellow, brassy glare of the sunshine, with the shadows of the palm trees as black and definite as the trees themselves </s>
<s> The air was calm, full of the eternal hum of insects, a tropical chorus of many octaves, from the deep drone of the bee to the high, keen pipe of the mosquito </s>
<s> Beyond the veranda was a small cleared garden, bounded with cactus hedges and adorned with clumps of flowering shrubs, round which the great blue butterflies and the tiny humming-birds fluttered and darted in crescents of sparkling light </s>
<s> Within we were seated round the cane table, on which lay a sealed envelope </s>
<s> Inscribed upon it, in the jagged handwriting of Professor Challenger, were the words:-- "Instructions to Lord John Roxton and party </s>

<s> Lord John had placed his watch upon the table beside him </s>
<s> "We have seven more minutes," said he </s>
<s> "The old dear is very precise" </s>

<s> So far as climate goes, it was immaterial what time we chose for our expedition, as the temperature ranges from seventy-five to ninety degrees both summer and winter, with no appreciable difference in heat </s>

<s> From the assurance of Professor Challenger's manner--and in spite of the continued scepticism of Professor Summerlee--I have no doubt that our leader will make good his statement, and that we are really on the eve of some most remarkable experiences </s>

<s> Vivid orchids and wonderful colored lichens smoldered upon the swarthy tree-trunks and where a wandering shaft of light fell full upon the golden allamanda, the scarlet star-clusters of the tacsonia, or the rich deep blue of ipomaea, the effect was as a dream of fairyland </s>

<s> The road still ascended, and we crossed a rock-studded slope which took two days to traverse </s>
<s> The vegetation had again changed, and only the vegetable ivory tree remained, with a great profusion of wonderful orchids, among which I learned to recognize the rare Nuttonia Vexillaria and the glorious pink and scarlet blossoms of Cattleya and odontoglossum </s>
<s> Occasional brooks with pebbly bottoms and fern-draped banks gurgled down the shallow gorges in the hill, and offered good camping-grounds every evening on the banks of some rock-studded pool, where swarms of little blue-backed fish, about the size and shape of English trout, gave us a delicious supper </s>
<s> On the ninth day after leaving the canoes, having done, as I reckon, about a hundred and twenty miles, we began to emerge from the trees, which had grown smaller until they were mere shrubs </s>
<s> Their place was taken by an immense wilderness of bamboo, which grew so thickly that we could only penetrate it by cutting a pathway with the machetes and billhooks of the Indians </s>
<s> It took us a long day, traveling from seven in the morning till eight at night, with only two breaks of one hour each, to get through this obstacle </s>
<s> Anything more monotonous and wearying could not be imagined, for, even at the most open places, I could not see more than ten or twelve yards, while usually my vision was limited to the back of Lord John's cotton jacket in front of me, and to the yellow wall within a foot of me on either side </s>
<s> From above came one thin knife-edge of sunshine, and fifteen feet over our heads one saw the tops of the reeds swaying against the deep blue sky </s>
<s> I do not know what kind of creatures inhabit such a thicket, but several times we heard the plunging of large, heavy animals quite close to us </s>
<s> From their sounds Lord John judged them to be some form of wild cattle </s>
<s> Just as night fell we cleared the belt of bamboos, and at once formed our camp, exhausted by the interminable day </s>
<s> Early next morning we were again afoot, and found that the character of the country had changed once again </s>
<s> Behind us was the wall of bamboo, as definite as if it marked the course of a river </s>
<s> In front was an open plain, sloping slightly upwards and dotted with clumps of tree-ferns, the whole curving before us until it ended in a long, whale-backed ridge </s>
<s> This we reached about midday, only to find a shallow valley beyond, rising once again into a gentle incline which led to a low, rounded sky-line </s>
<s> It was here, while we crossed the first of these hills, that an incident occurred which may or may not have been important </s>
<s> Professor Challenger, who with the two local Indians was in the van of the party, stopped suddenly and pointed excitedly to the right </s>
<s> As he did so we saw, at the distance of a mile or so, something which appeared to be a huge gray bird flap slowly up from the ground and skim smoothly off, flying very low and straight, until it was lost among the tree-ferns </s>
<s> "Did you see it" </s>
<s> cried Challenger, in exultation </s>
<s> "Summerlee, did you see it" </s>
<s> His colleague was staring at the spot where the creature had disappeared </s>
<s> "What do you claim that it was" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "To the best of my belief, a pterodactyl" </s>
<s> Summerlee burst into derisive laughter "A pter-fiddlestick" </s>
<s> said he </s>
<s> "It was a stork, if ever I saw one" </s>
<s> Challenger was too furious to speak </s>
<s> He simply swung his pack upon his back and continued upon his march </s>
<s> Lord John came abreast of me, however, and his face was more grave than was his wont </s>
<s> He had his Zeiss glasses in his hand </s>
<s> "I focused it before it got over the trees," said he </s>
<s> "I won't undertake to say what it was, but I'll risk my reputation as a sportsman that it wasn't any bird that ever I clapped eyes on in my life" </s>
<s> So there the matter stands </s>
<s> Are we really just at the edge of the unknown, encountering the outlying pickets of this lost world of which our leader speaks </s>
<s> I give you the incident as it occurred and you will know as much as I do </s>
<s> It stands alone, for we saw nothing more which could be called remarkable </s>
<s> And now, my readers, if ever I have any, I have brought you up the broad river, and through the screen of rushes, and down the green tunnel, and up the long slope of palm trees, and through the bamboo brake, and across the plain of tree-ferns </s>
<s> At last our destination lay in full sight of us </s>
<s> When we had crossed the second ridge we saw before us an irregular, palm-studded plain, and then the line of high red cliffs which I have seen in the picture </s>
<s> There it lies, even as I write, and there can be no question that it is the same </s>
<s> At the nearest point it is about seven miles from our present camp, and it curves away, stretching as far as I can see </s>
<s> Challenger struts about like a prize peacock, and Summerlee is silent, but still sceptical </s>
<s> Another day should bring some of our doubts to an end </s>
<s> Meanwhile, as Jose, whose arm was pierced by a broken bamboo, insists upon returning, I send this letter back in his charge, and only hope that it may eventually come to hand </s>
<s> I will write again as the occasion serves </s>
<s> I have enclosed with this a rough chart of our journey, which may have the effect of making the account rather easier to understand </s>
<s> CHAPTER IX "Who could have Foreseen it" </s>
<s> A dreadful thing has happened to us </s>
<s> Who could have foreseen it </s>
<s> I cannot foresee any end to our troubles </s>
<s> It may be that we are condemned to spend our whole lives in this strange, inaccessible place </s>
<s> I am still so confused that I can hardly think clearly of the facts of the present or of the chances of the future </s>
<s> To my astounded senses the one seems most terrible and the other as black as night </s>
<s> No men have ever found themselves in a worse position; nor is there any use in disclosing to you our exact geographical situation and asking our friends for a relief party </s>
<s> Even if they could send one, our fate will in all human probability be decided long before it could arrive in South America </s>
<s> We are, in truth, as far from any human aid as if we were in the moon </s>
<s> If we are to win through, it is only our own qualities which can save us </s>
<s> I have as companions three remarkable men, men of great brain-power and of unshaken courage </s>
<s> There lies our one and only hope </s>
<s> It is only when I look upon the untroubled faces of my comrades that I see some glimmer through the darkness </s>
<s> Outwardly I trust that I appear as unconcerned as they </s>
<s> Inwardly I am filled with apprehension </s>
<s> Let me give you, with as much detail as I can, the sequence of events which have led us to this catastrophe </s>
<s> When I finished my last letter I stated that we were within seven miles from an enormous line of ruddy cliffs, which encircled, beyond all doubt, the plateau of which Professor Challenger spoke </s>
<s> Their height, as we approached them, seemed to me in some places to be greater than he had stated--running up in parts to at least a thousand feet--and they were curiously striated, in a manner which is, I believe, characteristic of basaltic upheavals </s>
<s> Something of the sort is to be seen in Salisbury Crags at Edinburgh </s>
<s> The summit showed every sign of a luxuriant vegetation, with bushes near the edge, and farther back many high trees </s>
<s> There was no indication of any life that we could see </s>
<s> That night we pitched our camp immediately under the cliff--a most wild and desolate spot </s>
<s> The crags above us were not merely perpendicular, but curved outwards at the top, so that ascent was out of the question </s>
<s> Close to us was the high thin pinnacle of rock which I believe I mentioned earlier in this narrative </s>
<s> It is like a broad red church spire, the top of it being level with the plateau, but a great chasm gaping between </s>
<s> On the summit of it there grew one high tree </s>
<s> Both pinnacle and cliff were comparatively low--some five or six hundred feet, I should think </s>
<s> "It was on that," said Professor Challenger, pointing to this tree, "that the pterodactyl was perched </s>
<s> I climbed half-way up the rock before I shot him </s>
<s> I am inclined to think that a good mountaineer like myself could ascend the rock to the top, though he would, of course, be no nearer to the plateau when he had done so" </s>
<s> As Challenger spoke of his pterodactyl I glanced at Professor Summerlee, and for the first time I seemed to see some signs of a dawning credulity and repentance </s>
<s> There was no sneer upon his thin lips, but, on the contrary, a gray, drawn look of excitement and amazement </s>
<s> Challenger saw it, too, and reveled in the first taste of victory </s>
<s> "Of course," said he, with his clumsy and ponderous sarcasm, "Professor Summerlee will understand that when I speak of a pterodactyl I mean a stork--only it is the kind of stork which has no feathers, a leathery skin, membranous wings, and teeth in its jaws" </s>
<s> He grinned and blinked and bowed until his colleague turned and walked away </s>
<s> In the morning, after a frugal breakfast of coffee and manioc--we had to be economical of our stores--we held a council of war as to the best method of ascending to the plateau above us </s>
<s> Challenger presided with a solemnity as if he were the Lord Chief Justice on the Bench </s>
<s> Picture him seated upon a rock, his absurd boyish straw hat tilted on the back of his head, his supercilious eyes dominating us from under his drooping lids, his great black beard wagging as he slowly defined our present situation and our future movements </s>
<s> Beneath him you might have seen the three of us--myself, sunburnt, young, and vigorous after our open-air tramp; Summerlee, solemn but still critical, behind his eternal pipe; Lord John, as keen as a razor-edge, with his supple, alert figure leaning upon his rifle, and his eager eyes fixed eagerly upon the speaker </s>
<s> Behind us were grouped the two swarthy half-breeds and the little knot of Indians, while in front and above us towered those huge, ruddy ribs of rocks which kept us from our goal </s>
<s> "I need not say," said our leader, "that on the occasion of my last visit I exhausted every means of climbing the cliff, and where I failed I do not think that anyone else is likely to succeed, for I am something of a mountaineer </s>
<s> I had none of the appliances of a rock-climber with me, but I have taken the precaution to bring them now </s>
<s> With their aid I am positive I could climb that detached pinnacle to the summit; but so long as the main cliff overhangs, it is vain to attempt ascending that </s>
<s> I was hurried upon my last visit by the approach of the rainy season and by the exhaustion of my supplies </s>
<s> These considerations limited my time, and I can only claim that I have surveyed about six miles of the cliff to the east of us, finding no possible way up </s>
<s> What, then, shall we now do" </s>
<s> "There seems to be only one reasonable course," said Professor Summerlee </s>
<s> "If you have explored the east, we should travel along the base of the cliff to the west, and seek for a practicable point for our ascent" </s>
<s> "That's it," said Lord John </s>
<s> "The odds are that this plateau is of no great size, and we shall travel round it until we either find an easy way up it, or come back to the point from which we started" </s>
<s> "I have already explained to our young friend here," said Challenger (he has a way of alluding to me as if I were a school child ten years old), "that it is quite impossible that there should be an easy way up anywhere, for the simple reason that if there were the summit would not be isolated, and those conditions would not obtain which have effected so singular an interference with the general laws of survival </s>
<s> Yet I admit that there may very well be places where an expert human climber may reach the summit, and yet a cumbrous and heavy animal be unable to descend </s>
<s> It is certain that there is a point where an ascent is possible" </s>
<s> "How do you know that, sir" </s>
<s> asked Summerlee, sharply </s>
<s> "Because my predecessor, the American Maple White, actually made such an ascent </s>
<s> How otherwise could he have seen the monster which he sketched in his notebook" </s>
<s> "There you reason somewhat ahead of the proved facts," said the stubborn Summerlee </s>
<s> "I admit your plateau, because I have seen it; but I have not as yet satisfied myself that it contains any form of life whatever" </s>
<s> "What you admit, sir, or what you do not admit, is really of inconceivably small importance </s>
<s> I am glad to perceive that the plateau itself has actually obtruded itself upon your intelligence" </s>
<s> He glanced up at it, and then, to our amazement, he sprang from his rock, and, seizing Summerlee by the neck, he tilted his face into the air </s>
<s> "Now sir" </s>
<s> he shouted, hoarse with excitement </s>
<s> "Do I help you to realize that the plateau contains some animal life" </s>
<s> I have said that a thick fringe of green overhung the edge of the cliff </s>
<s> Out of this there had emerged a black, glistening object </s>
<s> As it came slowly forth and overhung the chasm, we saw that it was a very large snake with a peculiar flat, spade-like head </s>
<s> It wavered and quivered above us for a minute, the morning sun gleaming upon its sleek, sinuous coils </s>
<s> Then it slowly drew inwards and disappeared </s>
<s> Summerlee had been so interested that he had stood unresisting while Challenger tilted his head into the air </s>
<s> Now he shook his colleague off and came back to his dignity </s>
<s> "I should be glad, Professor Challenger," said he, "if you could see your way to make any remarks which may occur to you without seizing me by the chin </s>
<s> Even the appearance of a very ordinary rock python does not appear to justify such a liberty" </s>
<s> "But there is life upon the plateau all the same," his colleague replied in triumph </s>
<s> "And now, having demonstrated this important conclusion so that it is clear to anyone, however prejudiced or obtuse, I am of opinion that we cannot do better than break up our camp and travel to westward until we find some means of ascent" </s>
<s> The ground at the foot of the cliff was rocky and broken so that the going was slow and difficult </s>
<s> Suddenly we came, however, upon something which cheered our hearts </s>
<s> It was the site of an old encampment, with several empty Chicago meat tins, a bottle labeled "Brandy," a broken tin-opener, and a quantity of other travelers' debris </s>
<s> A crumpled, disintegrated newspaper revealed itself as the Chicago Democrat, though the date had been obliterated </s>
<s> "Not mine," said Challenger </s>
<s> "It must be Maple White's" </s>
<s> Lord John had been gazing curiously at a great tree-fern which overshadowed the encampment </s>
<s> "I say, look at this," said he </s>
<s> "I believe it is meant for a sign-post" </s>
<s> A slip of hard wood had been nailed to the tree in such a way as to point to the westward </s>
<s> "Most certainly a sign-post," said Challenger </s>
<s> "What else </s>
<s> Finding himself upon a dangerous errand, our pioneer has left this sign so that any party which follows him may know the way he has taken </s>
<s> Perhaps we shall come upon some other indications as we proceed" </s>
<s> We did indeed, but they were of a terrible and most unexpected nature </s>
<s> Immediately beneath the cliff there grew a considerable patch of high bamboo, like that which we had traversed in our journey </s>
<s> Many of these stems were twenty feet high, with sharp, strong tops, so that even as they stood they made formidable spears </s>
<s> We were passing along the edge of this cover when my eye was caught by the gleam of something white within it </s>
<s> Thrusting in my head between the stems, I found myself gazing at a fleshless skull </s>
<s> The whole skeleton was there, but the skull had detached itself and lay some feet nearer to the open </s>
<s> With a few blows from the machetes of our Indians we cleared the spot and were able to study the details of this old tragedy </s>
<s> Only a few shreds of clothes could still be distinguished, but there were the remains of boots upon the bony feet, and it was very clear that the dead man was a European </s>
<s> A gold watch by Hudson, of New York, and a chain which held a stylographic pen, lay among the bones </s>
<s> There was also a silver cigarette-case, with "J </s>
<s> C., from A </s>
<s> E </s>
<s> S.," upon the lid </s>
<s> The state of the metal seemed to show that the catastrophe had occurred no great time before </s>
<s> "Who can he be" </s>
<s> asked Lord John </s>
<s> "Poor devil </s>
<s> every bone in his body seems to be broken" </s>
<s> "And the bamboo grows through his smashed ribs," said Summerlee </s>
<s> "It is a fast-growing plant, but it is surely inconceivable that this body could have been here while the canes grew to be twenty feet in length" </s>
<s> "As to the man's identity," said Professor Challenger, "I have no doubt whatever upon that point </s>
<s> As I made my way up the river before I reached you at the fazenda I instituted very particular inquiries about Maple White </s>
<s> At Para they knew nothing </s>
<s> Fortunately, I had a definite clew, for there was a particular picture in his sketch-book which showed him taking lunch with a certain ecclesiastic at Rosario </s>
<s> This priest I was able to find, and though he proved a very argumentative fellow, who took it absurdly amiss that I should point out to him the corrosive effect which modern science must have upon his beliefs, he none the less gave me some positive information </s>
<s> Maple White passed Rosario four years ago, or two years before I saw his dead body </s>
<s> He was not alone at the time, but there was a friend, an American named James Colver, who remained in the boat and did not meet this ecclesiastic </s>
<s> I think, therefore, that there can be no doubt that we are now looking upon the remains of this James Colver" </s>
<s> "Nor," said Lord John, "is there much doubt as to how he met his death </s>
<s> He has fallen or been chucked from the top, and so been impaled </s>

<s> A hush came over us as we stood round these shattered remains and realized the truth of Lord John Roxton's words </s>
<s> The beetling head of the cliff projected over the cane-brake </s>
<s> Undoubtedly he had fallen from above </s>
<s> But had he fallen </s>
<s> Had it been an accident </s>
<s> Or--already ominous and terrible possibilities began to form round that unknown land </s>
<s> We moved off in silence, and continued to coast round the line of cliffs, which were as even and unbroken as some of those monstrous Antarctic ice-fields which I have seen depicted as stretching from horizon to horizon and towering high above the mast-heads of the exploring vessel </s>
<s> In five miles we saw no rift or break </s>
<s> And then suddenly we perceived something which filled us with new hope </s>
<s> In a hollow of the rock, protected from rain, there was drawn a rough arrow in chalk, pointing still to the westwards </s>
<s> "Maple White again," said Professor Challenger </s>
<s> "He had some presentiment that worthy footsteps would follow close behind him" </s>
<s> "He had chalk, then" </s>
<s> "A box of colored chalks was among the effects I found in his knapsack </s>
<s> I remember that the white one was worn to a stump" </s>
<s> "That is certainly good evidence," said Summerlee </s>
<s> "We can only accept his guidance and follow on to the westward" </s>
<s> We had proceeded some five more miles when again we saw a white arrow upon the rocks </s>
<s> It was at a point where the face of the cliff was for the first time split into a narrow cleft </s>
<s> Inside the cleft was a second guidance mark, which pointed right up it with the tip somewhat elevated, as if the spot indicated were above the level of the ground </s>
<s> It was a solemn place, for the walls were so gigantic and the slit of blue sky so narrow and so obscured by a double fringe of verdure, that only a dim and shadowy light penetrated to the bottom </s>
<s> We had had no food for many hours, and were very weary with the stony and irregular journey, but our nerves were too strung to allow us to halt </s>
<s> We ordered the camp to be pitched, however, and, leaving the Indians to arrange it, we four, with the two half-breeds, proceeded up the narrow gorge </s>
<s> It was not more than forty feet across at the mouth, but it rapidly closed until it ended in an acute angle, too straight and smooth for an ascent </s>
<s> Certainly it was not this which our pioneer had attempted to indicate </s>
<s> We made our way back--the whole gorge was not more than a quarter of a mile deep--and then suddenly the quick eyes of Lord John fell upon what we were seeking </s>
<s> High up above our heads, amid the dark shadows, there was one circle of deeper gloom </s>
<s> Surely it could only be the opening of a cave </s>
<s> The base of the cliff was heaped with loose stones at the spot, and it was not difficult to clamber up </s>
<s> When we reached it, all doubt was removed </s>
<s> Not only was it an opening into the rock, but on the side of it there was marked once again the sign of the arrow </s>
<s> Here was the point, and this the means by which Maple White and his ill-fated comrade had made their ascent </s>
<s> We were too excited to return to the camp, but must make our first exploration at once </s>
<s> Lord John had an electric torch in his knapsack, and this had to serve us as light </s>
<s> He advanced, throwing his little clear circlet of yellow radiance before him, while in single file we followed at his heels </s>
<s> The cave had evidently been water-worn, the sides being smooth and the floor covered with rounded stones </s>
<s> It was of such a size that a single man could just fit through by stooping </s>
<s> For fifty yards it ran almost straight into the rock, and then it ascended at an angle of forty-five </s>
<s> Presently this incline became even steeper, and we found ourselves climbing upon hands and knees among loose rubble which slid from beneath us </s>
<s> Suddenly an exclamation broke from Lord Roxton </s>
<s> "It's blocked" </s>
<s> said he </s>
<s> Clustering behind him we saw in the yellow field of light a wall of broken basalt which extended to the ceiling </s>
<s> "The roof has fallen in" </s>
<s> In vain we dragged out some of the pieces </s>
<s> The only effect was that the larger ones became detached and threatened to roll down the gradient and crush us </s>
<s> It was evident that the obstacle was far beyond any efforts which we could make to remove it </s>
<s> The road by which Maple White had ascended was no longer available </s>
<s> Too much cast down to speak, we stumbled down the dark tunnel and made our way back to the camp </s>
<s> One incident occurred, however, before we left the gorge, which is of importance in view of what came afterwards </s>
<s> We had gathered in a little group at the bottom of the chasm, some forty feet beneath the mouth of the cave, when a huge rock rolled suddenly downwards--and shot past us with tremendous force </s>
<s> It was the narrowest escape for one or all of us </s>
<s> We could not ourselves see whence the rock had come, but our half-breed servants, who were still at the opening of the cave, said that it had flown past them, and must therefore have fallen from the summit </s>
<s> Looking upwards, we could see no sign of movement above us amidst the green jungle which topped the cliff </s>
<s> There could be little doubt, however, that the stone was aimed at us, so the incident surely pointed to humanity--and malevolent humanity--upon the plateau </s>
<s> We withdrew hurriedly from the chasm, our minds full of this new development and its bearing upon our plans </s>
<s> The situation was difficult enough before, but if the obstructions of Nature were increased by the deliberate opposition of man, then our case was indeed a hopeless one </s>
<s> And yet, as we looked up at that beautiful fringe of verdure only a few hundreds of feet above our heads, there was not one of us who could conceive the idea of returning to London until we had explored it to its depths </s>
<s> On discussing the situation, we determined that our best course was to continue to coast round the plateau in the hope of finding some other means of reaching the top </s>
<s> The line of cliffs, which had decreased considerably in height, had already begun to trend from west to north, and if we could take this as representing the arc of a circle, the whole circumference could not be very great </s>
<s> At the worst, then, we should be back in a few days at our starting-point </s>
<s> We made a march that day which totaled some two-and-twenty miles, without any change in our prospects </s>
<s> I may mention that our aneroid shows us that in the continual incline which we have ascended since we abandoned our canoes we have risen to no less than three thousand feet above sea-level </s>
<s> Hence there is a considerable change both in the temperature and in the vegetation </s>
<s> We have shaken off some of that horrible insect life which is the bane of tropical travel </s>
<s> A few palms still survive, and many tree-ferns, but the Amazonian trees have been all left behind </s>
<s> It was pleasant to see the convolvulus, the passion-flower, and the begonia, all reminding me of home, here among these inhospitable rocks </s>
<s> There was a red begonia just the same color as one that is kept in a pot in the window of a certain villa in Streatham--but I am drifting into private reminiscence </s>
<s> That night--I am still speaking of the first day of our circumnavigation of the plateau--a great experience awaited us, and one which for ever set at rest any doubt which we could have had as to the wonders so near us </s>
<s> You will realize as you read it, my dear Mr McArdle, and possibly for the first time that the paper has not sent me on a wild-goose chase, and that there is inconceivably fine copy waiting for the world whenever we have the Professor's leave to make use of it </s>
<s> I shall not dare to publish these articles unless I can bring back my proofs to England, or I shall be hailed as the journalistic Munchausen of all time </s>
<s> I have no doubt that you feel the same way yourself, and that you would not care to stake the whole credit of the Gazette upon this adventure until we can meet the chorus of criticism and scepticism which such articles must of necessity elicit </s>
<s> So this wonderful incident, which would make such a headline for the old paper, must still wait its turn in the editorial drawer </s>
<s> And yet it was all over in a flash, and there was no sequel to it, save in our own convictions </s>
<s> What occurred was this </s>
<s> Lord John had shot an ajouti--which is a small, pig-like animal--and, half of it having been given to the Indians, we were cooking the other half upon our fire </s>
<s> There is a chill in the air after dark, and we had all drawn close to the blaze </s>
<s> The night was moonless, but there were some stars, and one could see for a little distance across the plain </s>
<s> Well, suddenly out of the darkness, out of the night, there swooped something with a swish like an aeroplane </s>
<s> The whole group of us were covered for an instant by a canopy of leathery wings, and I had a momentary vision of a long, snake-like neck, a fierce, red, greedy eye, and a great snapping beak, filled, to my amazement, with little, gleaming teeth </s>
<s> The next instant it was gone--and so was our dinner </s>
<s> A huge black shadow, twenty feet across, skimmed up into the air; for an instant the monster wings blotted out the stars, and then it vanished over the brow of the cliff above us </s>
<s> We all sat in amazed silence round the fire, like the heroes of Virgil when the Harpies came down upon them </s>
<s> It was Summerlee who was the first to speak </s>
<s> "Professor Challenger," said he, in a solemn voice, which quavered with emotion, "I owe you an apology </s>
<s> Sir, I am very much in the wrong, and I beg that you will forget what is past" </s>
<s> It was handsomely said, and the two men for the first time shook hands </s>
<s> So much we have gained by this clear vision of our first pterodactyl </s>
<s> It was worth a stolen supper to bring two such men together </s>
<s> But if prehistoric life existed upon the plateau it was not superabundant, for we had no further glimpse of it during the next three days </s>
<s> During this time we traversed a barren and forbidding country, which alternated between stony desert and desolate marshes full of many wild-fowl, upon the north and east of the cliffs </s>
<s> From that direction the place is really inaccessible, and, were it not for a hardish ledge which runs at the very base of the precipice, we should have had to turn back </s>

<s> CHAPTER X "The most Wonderful Things have Happened" The most wonderful things have happened and are continually happening to us </s>
<s> All the paper that I possess consists of five old note-books and a lot of scraps, and I have only the one stylographic pencil; but so long as I can move my hand I will continue to set down our experiences and impressions, for, since we are the only men of the whole human race to see such things, it is of enormous importance that I should record them whilst they are fresh in my memory and before that fate which seems to be constantly impending does actually overtake us </s>
<s> Whether Zambo can at last take these letters to the river, or whether I shall myself in some miraculous way carry them back with me, or, finally, whether some daring explorer, coming upon our tracks with the advantage, perhaps, of a perfected monoplane, should find this bundle of manuscript, in any case I can see that what I am writing is destined to immortality as a classic of true adventure </s>
<s> On the morning after our being trapped upon the plateau by the villainous Gomez we began a new stage in our experiences </s>
<s> The first incident in it was not such as to give me a very favorable opinion of the place to which we had wandered </s>

<s> Zambo occupied our little tent at the base of the pinnacle, and there he remained, our one link with the world below </s>
<s> And now we had to decide upon our immediate movements </s>
<s> We shifted our position from among the tick-laden bushes until we came to a small clearing thickly surrounded by trees upon all sides </s>
<s> There were some flat slabs of rock in the center, with an excellent well close by, and there we sat in cleanly comfort while we made our first plans for the invasion of this new country </s>
<s> Birds were calling among the foliage--especially one with a peculiar whooping cry which was new to us--but beyond these sounds there were no signs of life </s>
<s> Our first care was to make some sort of list of our own stores, so that we might know what we had to rely upon </s>
<s> What with the things we had ourselves brought up and those which Zambo had sent across on the rope, we were fairly well supplied </s>
<s> Most important of all, in view of the dangers which might surround us, we had our four rifles and one thousand three hundred rounds, also a shot-gun, but not more than a hundred and fifty medium pellet cartridges </s>
<s> In the matter of provisions we had enough to last for several weeks, with a sufficiency of tobacco and a few scientific implements, including a large telescope and a good field-glass </s>
<s> All these things we collected together in the clearing, and as a first precaution, we cut down with our hatchet and knives a number of thorny bushes, which we piled round in a circle some fifteen yards in diameter </s>

<s> It was midday before we had made ourselves secure, but the heat was not oppressive, and the general character of the plateau, both in its temperature and in its vegetation, was almost temperate </s>

<s> In its shade we continued our discussion, while Lord John, who had quickly taken command in the hour of action, gave us his views </s>
<s> "So long as neither man nor beast has seen or heard us, we are safe," said he </s>
<s> "From the time they know we are here our troubles begin </s>
<s> There are no signs that they have found us out as yet </s>

<s> "By all means, sonny my boy </s>
<s> We will advance </s>
<s> But with common sense </s>
<s> We must never go so far that we can't get back to our base </s>

<s> "Well, it couldn't be helped </s>

<s> The peaceful penetration of Maple White Land was the pressing subject before us </s>
<s> We had the evidence of our own eyes that the place was inhabited by some unknown creatures, and there was that of Maple White's sketch-book to show that more dreadful and more dangerous monsters might still appear </s>

<s> Our situation, stranded without possibility of escape in such a land, was clearly full of danger, and our reasons endorsed every measure of caution which Lord John's experience could suggest </s>

<s> We therefore blocked the entrance to our zareba by filling it up with several thorny bushes, and left our camp with the stores entirely surrounded by this protecting hedge </s>

<s> said he </s>

<s> A strong wind blew towards us and we were well concealed, so there was no chance of discovery </s>

<s> I looked at my comrades </s>
<s> Lord John was standing at gaze with his finger on the trigger of his elephant-gun, his eager hunter's soul shining from his fierce eyes </s>

<s> "Nunc dimittis" </s>

<s> I had the same feeling of mystery and danger around us </s>
<s> In the gloom of the trees there seemed a constant menace and as we looked up into their shadowy foliage vague terrors crept into one's heart </s>
<s> It is true that these monstrous creatures which we had seen were lumbering, inoffensive brutes which were unlikely to hurt anyone, but in this world of wonders what other survivals might there not be--what fierce, active horrors ready to pounce upon us from their lair among the rocks or brushwood </s>
<s> I knew little of prehistoric life, but I had a clear remembrance of one book which I had read in which it spoke of creatures who would live upon our lions and tigers as a cat lives upon mice </s>

<s> It was a loathsome adventure, and one of which I hate to think </s>
<s> If, as Lord John said, the glade of the iguanodons will remain with us as a dream, then surely the swamp of the pterodactyls will forever be our nightmare </s>
<s> Let me set down exactly what occurred </s>
<s> We passed very slowly through the woods, partly because Lord Roxton acted as scout before he would let us advance, and partly because at every second step one or other of our professors would fall, with a cry of wonder, before some flower or insect which presented him with a new type </s>
<s> We may have traveled two or three miles in all, keeping to the right of the line of the stream, when we came upon a considerable opening in the trees </s>
<s> A belt of brushwood led up to a tangle of rocks--the whole plateau was strewn with boulders </s>
<s> We were walking slowly towards these rocks, among bushes which reached over our waists, when we became aware of a strange low gabbling and whistling sound, which filled the air with a constant clamor and appeared to come from some spot immediately before us </s>
<s> Lord John held up his hand as a signal for us to stop, and he made his way swiftly, stooping and running, to the line of rocks </s>

<s> Finally he waved us to come on, holding up his hand as a signal for caution </s>

<s> Creeping to his side, we looked over the rocks </s>
<s> The place into which we gazed was a pit, and may, in the early days, have been one of the smaller volcanic blow-holes of the plateau </s>
<s> It was bowl-shaped and at the bottom, some hundreds of yards from where we lay, were pools of green-scummed, stagnant water, fringed with bullrushes </s>
<s> It was a weird place in itself, but its occupants made it seem like a scene from the Seven Circles of Dante </s>
<s> The place was a rookery of pterodactyls </s>
<s> There were hundreds of them congregated within view </s>
<s> All the bottom area round the water-edge was alive with their young ones, and with hideous mothers brooding upon their leathery, yellowish eggs </s>

<s> But above, perched each upon its own stone, tall, gray, and withered, more like dead and dried specimens than actual living creatures, sat the horrible males, absolutely motionless save for the rolling of their red eyes or an occasional snap of their rat-trap beaks as a dragon-fly went past them </s>
<s> Their huge, membranous wings were closed by folding their fore-arms, so that they sat like gigantic old women, wrapped in hideous web-colored shawls, and with their ferocious heads protruding above them </s>

<s> "The brutes mean mischief" </s>

<s> Then suddenly out of the whizzing, slate-colored circle a long neck shot out, and a fierce beak made a thrust at us </s>

<s> Summerlee gave a cry and put his hand to his face, from which the blood was streaming </s>
<s> I felt a prod at the back of my neck, and turned dizzy with the shock </s>

<s> The gate of Fort Challenger had been untouched, the walls were unbroken, and yet it had been visited by some strange and powerful creature in our absence </s>

<s> "All well, Massa Challenger, all well" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "Me stay here </s>
<s> No fear </s>

<s> His honest black face, and the immense view before us, which carried us half-way back to the affluent of the Amazon, helped us to remember that we really were upon this earth in the twentieth century, and had not by some magic been conveyed to some raw planet in its earliest and wildest state </s>

<s> The two professors, their tempers aggravated no doubt by their injuries, had fallen out as to whether our assailants were of the genus pterodactylus or dimorphodon, and high words had ensued </s>
<s> To avoid their wrangling I moved some little way apart, and was seated smoking upon the trunk of a fallen tree, when Lord John strolled over in my direction </s>
<s> "I say, Malone," said he, "do you remember that place where those beasts were" </s>
<s> "Very clearly" </s>
<s> "A sort of volcanic pit, was it not" </s>
<s> "Exactly," said I </s>
<s> "Did you notice the soil" </s>
<s> "Rocks" </s>
<s> "But round the water--where the reeds were" </s>

<s> "Exactly </s>

<s> "What of that" </s>

<s> They were the last words I heard before I dropped into an exhausted sleep </s>
<s> CHAPTER XI "For once I was the Hero" Lord John Roxton was right when he thought that some specially toxic quality might lie in the bite of the horrible creatures which had attacked us </s>
<s> On the morning after our first adventure upon the plateau, both Summerlee and I were in great pain and fever, while Challenger's knee was so bruised that he could hardly limp </s>
<s> We kept to our camp all day, therefore, Lord John busying himself, with such help as we could give him, in raising the height and thickness of the thorny walls which were our only defense </s>
<s> I remember that during the whole long day I was haunted by the feeling that we were closely observed, though by whom or whence I could give no guess </s>
<s> So strong was the impression that I told Professor Challenger of it, who put it down to the cerebral excitement caused by my fever </s>
<s> Again and again I glanced round swiftly, with the conviction that I was about to see something, but only to meet the dark tangle of our hedge or the solemn and cavernous gloom of the great trees which arched above our heads </s>
<s> And yet the feeling grew ever stronger in my own mind that something observant and something malevolent was at our very elbow </s>
<s> I thought of the Indian superstition of the Curupuri--the dreadful, lurking spirit of the woods--and I could have imagined that his terrible presence haunted those who had invaded his most remote and sacred retreat </s>
<s> That night (our third in Maple White Land) we had an experience which left a fearful impression upon our minds, and made us thankful that Lord John had worked so hard in making our retreat impregnable </s>
<s> We were all sleeping round our dying fire when we were aroused--or, rather, I should say, shot out of our slumbers--by a succession of the most frightful cries and screams to which I have ever listened </s>
<s> I know no sound to which I could compare this amazing tumult, which seemed to come from some spot within a few hundred yards of our camp </s>
<s> It was as ear-splitting as any whistle of a railway-engine; but whereas the whistle is a clear, mechanical, sharp-edged sound, this was far deeper in volume and vibrant with the uttermost strain of agony and horror </s>
<s> We clapped our hands to our ears to shut out that nerve-shaking appeal </s>
<s> A cold sweat broke out over my body, and my heart turned sick at the misery of it </s>
<s> All the woes of tortured life, all its stupendous indictment of high heaven, its innumerable sorrows, seemed to be centered and condensed into that one dreadful, agonized cry </s>
<s> And then, under this high-pitched, ringing sound there was another, more intermittent, a low, deep-chested laugh, a growling, throaty gurgle of merriment which formed a grotesque accompaniment to the shriek with which it was blended </s>
<s> For three or four minutes on end the fearsome duet continued, while all the foliage rustled with the rising of startled birds </s>
<s> Then it shut off as suddenly as it began </s>
<s> For a long time we sat in horrified silence </s>
<s> Then Lord John threw a bundle of twigs upon the fire, and their red glare lit up the intent faces of my companions and flickered over the great boughs above our heads </s>
<s> "What was it" </s>
<s> I whispered </s>
<s> "We shall know in the morning," said Lord John </s>
<s> "It was close to us--not farther than the glade" </s>
<s> "We have been privileged to overhear a prehistoric tragedy, the sort of drama which occurred among the reeds upon the border of some Jurassic lagoon, when the greater dragon pinned the lesser among the slime," said Challenger, with more solemnity than I had ever heard in his voice </s>
<s> "It was surely well for man that he came late in the order of creation </s>
<s> There were powers abroad in earlier days which no courage and no mechanism of his could have met </s>

<s> CHAPTER XII "It was Dreadful in the Forest" I have said--or perhaps I have not said, for my memory plays me sad tricks these days--that I glowed with pride when three such men as my comrades thanked me for having saved, or at least greatly helped, the situation </s>
<s> As the youngster of the party, not merely in years, but in experience, character, knowledge, and all that goes to make a man, I had been overshadowed from the first </s>
<s> And now I was coming into my own </s>
<s> I warmed at the thought </s>
<s> Alas </s>
<s> for the pride which goes before a fall </s>
<s> That little glow of self-satisfaction, that added measure of self-confidence, were to lead me on that very night to the most dreadful experience of my life, ending with a shock which turns my heart sick when I think of it </s>
<s> It came about in this way </s>
<s> I had been unduly excited by the adventure of the tree, and sleep seemed to be impossible </s>
<s> Summerlee was on guard, sitting hunched over our small fire, a quaint, angular figure, his rifle across his knees and his pointed, goat-like beard wagging with each weary nod of his head </s>
<s> Lord John lay silent, wrapped in the South American poncho which he wore, while Challenger snored with a roll and rattle which reverberated through the woods </s>
<s> The full moon was shining brightly, and the air was crisply cold </s>
<s> What a night for a walk </s>
<s> And then suddenly came the thought, "Why not" </s>
<s> Suppose I stole softly away, suppose I made my way down to the central lake, suppose I was back at breakfast with some record of the place--would I not in that case be thought an even more worthy associate </s>
<s> Then, if Summerlee carried the day and some means of escape were found, we should return to London with first-hand knowledge of the central mystery of the plateau, to which I alone, of all men, would have penetrated </s>
<s> I thought of Gladys, with her "There are heroisms all round us" </s>
<s> I seemed to hear her voice as she said it </s>
<s> I thought also of McArdle </s>
<s> What a three column article for the paper </s>
<s> What a foundation for a career </s>
<s> A correspondentship in the next great war might be within my reach </s>
<s> I clutched at a gun--my pockets were full of cartridges--and, parting the thorn bushes at the gate of our zareba, quickly slipped out </s>
<s> My last glance showed me the unconscious Summerlee, most futile of sentinels, still nodding away like a queer mechanical toy in front of the smouldering fire </s>
<s> I had not gone a hundred yards before I deeply repented my rashness </s>
<s> I may have said somewhere in this chronicle that I am too imaginative to be a really courageous man, but that I have an overpowering fear of seeming afraid </s>
<s> This was the power which now carried me onwards </s>
<s> I simply could not slink back with nothing done </s>
<s> Even if my comrades should not have missed me, and should never know of my weakness, there would still remain some intolerable self-shame in my own soul </s>
<s> And yet I shuddered at the position in which I found myself, and would have given all I possessed at that moment to have been honorably free of the whole business </s>
<s> It was dreadful in the forest </s>
<s> The trees grew so thickly and their foliage spread so widely that I could see nothing of the moon-light save that here and there the high branches made a tangled filigree against the starry sky </s>
<s> As the eyes became more used to the obscurity one learned that there were different degrees of darkness among the trees--that some were dimly visible, while between and among them there were coal-black shadowed patches, like the mouths of caves, from which I shrank in horror as I passed </s>
<s> I thought of the despairing yell of the tortured iguanodon--that dreadful cry which had echoed through the woods </s>
<s> I thought, too, of the glimpse I had in the light of Lord John's torch of that bloated, warty, blood-slavering muzzle </s>
<s> Even now I was on its hunting-ground </s>
<s> At any instant it might spring upon me from the shadows--this nameless and horrible monster </s>
<s> I stopped, and, picking a cartridge from my pocket, I opened the breech of my gun </s>
<s> As I touched the lever my heart leaped within me </s>
<s> It was the shot-gun, not the rifle, which I had taken </s>
<s> Again the impulse to return swept over me </s>
<s> Here, surely, was a most excellent reason for my failure--one for which no one would think the less of me </s>
<s> But again the foolish pride fought against that very word </s>
<s> I could not--must not--fail </s>
<s> After all, my rifle would probably have been as useless as a shot-gun against such dangers as I might meet </s>
<s> If I were to go back to camp to change my weapon I could hardly expect to enter and to leave again without being seen </s>
<s> In that case there would be explanations, and my attempt would no longer be all my own </s>
<s> After a little hesitation, then, I screwed up my courage and continued upon my way, my useless gun under my arm </s>
<s> The darkness of the forest had been alarming, but even worse was the white, still flood of moonlight in the open glade of the iguanodons </s>
<s> Hid among the bushes, I looked out at it </s>
<s> None of the great brutes were in sight </s>
<s> Perhaps the tragedy which had befallen one of them had driven them from their feeding-ground </s>
<s> In the misty, silvery night I could see no sign of any living thing </s>
<s> Taking courage, therefore, I slipped rapidly across it, and among the jungle on the farther side I picked up once again the brook which was my guide </s>
<s> It was a cheery companion, gurgling and chuckling as it ran, like the dear old trout-stream in the West Country where I have fished at night in my boyhood </s>
<s> So long as I followed it down I must come to the lake, and so long as I followed it back I must come to the camp </s>
<s> Often I had to lose sight of it on account of the tangled brush-wood, but I was always within earshot of its tinkle and splash </s>
<s> As one descended the slope the woods became thinner, and bushes, with occasional high trees, took the place of the forest </s>
<s> I could make good progress, therefore, and I could see without being seen </s>
<s> I passed close to the pterodactyl swamp, and as I did so, with a dry, crisp, leathery rattle of wings, one of these great creatures--it was twenty feet at least from tip to tip--rose up from somewhere near me and soared into the air </s>
<s> As it passed across the face of the moon the light shone clearly through the membranous wings, and it looked like a flying skeleton against the white, tropical radiance </s>
<s> I crouched low among the bushes, for I knew from past experience that with a single cry the creature could bring a hundred of its loathsome mates about my ears </s>
<s> It was not until it had settled again that I dared to steal onwards upon my journey </s>
<s> The night had been exceedingly still, but as I advanced I became conscious of a low, rumbling sound, a continuous murmur, somewhere in front of me </s>
<s> This grew louder as I proceeded, until at last it was clearly quite close to me </s>
<s> When I stood still the sound was constant, so that it seemed to come from some stationary cause </s>
<s> It was like a boiling kettle or the bubbling of some great pot </s>
<s> Soon I came upon the source of it, for in the center of a small clearing I found a lake--or a pool, rather, for it was not larger than the basin of the Trafalgar Square fountain--of some black, pitch-like stuff, the surface of which rose and fell in great blisters of bursting gas </s>
<s> The air above it was shimmering with heat, and the ground round was so hot that I could hardly bear to lay my hand on it </s>
<s> It was clear that the great volcanic outburst which had raised this strange plateau so many years ago had not yet entirely spent its forces </s>
<s> Blackened rocks and mounds of lava I had already seen everywhere peeping out from amid the luxuriant vegetation which draped them, but this asphalt pool in the jungle was the first sign that we had of actual existing activity on the slopes of the ancient crater </s>
<s> I had no time to examine it further for I had need to hurry if I were to be back in camp in the morning </s>
<s> It was a fearsome walk, and one which will be with me so long as memory holds </s>
<s> In the great moonlight clearings I slunk along among the shadows on the margin </s>
<s> In the jungle I crept forward, stopping with a beating heart whenever I heard, as I often did, the crash of breaking branches as some wild beast went past </s>

<s> How often I stopped with the intention of returning, and yet every time my pride conquered my fear, and sent me on again until my object should be attained </s>
<s> At last (my watch showed that it was one in the morning) I saw the gleam of water amid the openings of the jungle, and ten minutes later I was among the reeds upon the borders of the central lake </s>
<s> I was exceedingly dry, so I lay down and took a long draught of its waters, which were fresh and cold </s>
<s> There was a broad pathway with many tracks upon it at the spot which I had found, so that it was clearly one of the drinking-places of the animals </s>
<s> Close to the water's edge there was a huge isolated block of lava </s>
<s> Up this I climbed, and, lying on the top, I had an excellent view in every direction </s>
<s> The first thing which I saw filled me with amazement </s>
<s> When I described the view from the summit of the great tree, I said that on the farther cliff I could see a number of dark spots, which appeared to be the mouths of caves </s>
<s> Now, as I looked up at the same cliffs, I saw discs of light in every direction, ruddy, clearly-defined patches, like the port-holes of a liner in the darkness </s>
<s> For a moment I thought it was the lava-glow from some volcanic action; but this could not be so </s>
<s> Any volcanic action would surely be down in the hollow and not high among the rocks </s>
<s> What, then, was the alternative </s>
<s> It was wonderful, and yet it must surely be </s>
<s> These ruddy spots must be the reflection of fires within the caves--fires which could only be lit by the hand of man </s>
<s> There were human beings, then, upon the plateau </s>
<s> How gloriously my expedition was justified </s>
<s> Here was news indeed for us to bear back with us to London </s>
<s> For a long time I lay and watched these red, quivering blotches of light </s>
<s> I suppose they were ten miles off from me, yet even at that distance one could observe how, from time to time, they twinkled or were obscured as someone passed before them </s>
<s> What would I not have given to be able to crawl up to them, to peep in, and to take back some word to my comrades as to the appearance and character of the race who lived in so strange a place </s>
<s> It was out of the question for the moment, and yet surely we could not leave the plateau until we had some definite knowledge upon the point </s>
<s> Lake Gladys--my own lake--lay like a sheet of quicksilver before me, with a reflected moon shining brightly in the center of it </s>
<s> It was shallow, for in many places I saw low sandbanks protruding above the water </s>

<s> Looking at my watch, I saw that it was half-past two o'clock, and high time, therefore, that I started upon my homeward journey </s>
<s> There was no difficulty about the direction in which I should return for all along I had kept the little brook upon my left, and it opened into the central lake within a stone's-throw of the boulder upon which I had been lying </s>
<s> I set off, therefore, in high spirits, for I felt that I had done good work and was bringing back a fine budget of news for my companions </s>
<s> Foremost of all, of course, were the sight of the fiery caves and the certainty that some troglodytic race inhabited them </s>
<s> But besides that I could speak from experience of the central lake </s>
<s> I could testify that it was full of strange creatures, and I had seen several land forms of primeval life which we had not before encountered </s>
<s> I reflected as I walked that few men in the world could have spent a stranger night or added more to human knowledge in the course of it </s>

<s> Some strange creature was evidently near me, but nothing could be seen, so I hastened more rapidly upon my way </s>
<s> I had traversed half a mile or so when suddenly the sound was repeated, still behind me, but louder and more menacing than before </s>
<s> My heart stood still within me as it flashed across me that the beast, whatever it was, must surely be after ME </s>
<s> My skin grew cold and my hair rose at the thought </s>
<s> That these monsters should tear each other to pieces was a part of the strange struggle for existence, but that they should turn upon modern man, that they should deliberately track and hunt down the predominant human, was a staggering and fearsome thought </s>

<s> Striking one of them, I was able at last to form some opinion of this place into which I had fallen </s>

<s> The post in the center, some nine feet long, was sharpened at the upper end, and was black with the stale blood of the creatures who had been impaled upon it </s>

<s> To lie in wait for me now would mean that the creature had appreciated what had happened to me, and this in turn would argue some power connecting cause and effect </s>

<s> I clambered to the edge of the pit and looked over </s>

<s> I could see or hear nothing of my enemy </s>

<s> Some distance down it I picked up my gun, and shortly afterwards struck the brook which was my guide </s>
<s> So, with many a frightened backward glance, I made for home </s>

<s> For a moment I was shocked at the thought that some sudden danger might have befallen them </s>
<s> But then a simpler and more natural explanation came to my mind </s>
<s> It was now broad daylight </s>
<s> No doubt my absence had been noticed </s>
<s> They had imagined, that I was lost in the woods, and had fired this shot to guide me home </s>
<s> It is true that we had made a strict resolution against firing, but if it seemed to them that I might be in danger they would not hesitate </s>
<s> It was for me now to hurry on as fast as possible, and so to reassure them </s>
<s> I was weary and spent, so my progress was not so fast as I wished; but at last I came into regions which I knew </s>
<s> There was the swamp of the pterodactyls upon my left; there in front of me was the glade of the iguanodons </s>
<s> Now I was in the last belt of trees which separated me from Fort Challenger </s>
<s> I raised my voice in a cheery shout to allay their fears </s>
<s> No answering greeting came back to me </s>
<s> My heart sank at that ominous stillness </s>
<s> I quickened my pace into a run </s>
<s> The zareba rose before me, even as I had left it, but the gate was open </s>
<s> I rushed in </s>
<s> In the cold, morning light it was a fearful sight which met my eyes </s>
<s> Our effects were scattered in wild confusion over the ground; my comrades had disappeared, and close to the smouldering ashes of our fire the grass was stained crimson with a hideous pool of blood </s>
